傅里叶级数

发表于 2019-04-29 | 分类于 数学

傅立叶级数、傅立叶变换实际上就是线性组合。

1 对周期函数进行分解的猜想

拉格朗日等数学家发现某些周期函数可以由三角函数的和来表示，比如下图中，黑色的斜线就是周期为%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mn%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMAIN-32%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%20transform%3D%22translate(500%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-3C0%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)的函数，而红色的曲线是三角函数之和，可以看出两者确实近似：

而另外一位数学家：

让·巴普蒂斯·约瑟夫·傅里叶男爵（1768 －1830）猜测任意周期函数都可以写成三角函数之和。

2 分解的思路

假设%3C%2Ftitle%3E%0A%3Cdefs%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-66%22%20d%3D%22M118%20-162Q120%20-162%20124%20-164T135%20-167T147%20-168Q160%20-168%20171%20-155T187%20-126Q197%20-99%20221%2027T267%20267T289%20382V385H242Q195%20385%20192%20387Q188%20390%20188%20397L195%20425Q197%20430%20203%20430T250%20431Q298%20431%20298%20432Q298%20434%20307%20482T319%20540Q356%20705%20465%20705Q502%20703%20526%20683T550%20630Q550%20594%20529%20578T487%20561Q443%20561%20443%20603Q443%20622%20454%20636T478%20657L487%20662Q471%20668%20457%20668Q445%20668%20434%20658T419%20630Q412%20601%20403%20552T387%20469T380%20433Q380%20431%20435%20431Q480%20431%20487%20430T498%20424Q499%20420%20496%20407T491%20391Q489%20386%20482%20386T428%20385H372L349%20263Q301%2015%20282%20-47Q255%20-132%20212%20-173Q175%20-205%20139%20-205Q107%20-205%2081%20-186T55%20-132Q55%20-95%2076%20-78T118%20-61Q162%20-61%20162%20-103Q162%20-122%20151%20-136T127%20-157L118%20-162Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMAIN-28%22%20d%3D%22M94%20250Q94%20319%20104%20381T127%20488T164%20576T202%20643T244%20695T277%20729T302%20750H315H319Q333%20750%20333%20741Q333%20738%20316%20720T275%20667T226%20581T184%20443T167%20250T184%2058T225%20-81T274%20-167T316%20-220T333%20-241Q333%20-250%20318%20-250H315H302L274%20-226Q180%20-141%20137%20-14T94%20250Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-78%22%20d%3D%22M52%20289Q59%20331%20106%20386T222%20442Q257%20442%20286%20424T329%20379Q371%20442%20430%20442Q467%20442%20494%20420T522%20361Q522%20332%20508%20314T481%20292T458%20288Q439%20288%20427%20299T415%20328Q415%20374%20465%20391Q454%20404%20425%20404Q412%20404%20406%20402Q368%20386%20350%20336Q290%20115%20290%2078Q290%2050%20306%2038T341%2026Q378%2026%20414%2059T463%20140Q466%20150%20469%20151T485%20153H489Q504%20153%20504%20145Q504%20144%20502%20134Q486%2077%20440%2033T333%20-11Q263%20-11%20227%2052Q186%20-10%20133%20-1 2%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-66%22%20d%3D%22M118%20-162Q120%20-162%20124%20-164T135%20-167T147%20-168Q160%20-168%20171%20-155T187%20-126Q197%20-99%20221%2027T267%20267T289%20382V385H242Q195%20385%20192%20387Q188%20390%20188%20397L195%20425Q197%20430%20203%20430T250%20431Q298%20431%20298%20432Q298%20434%20307%20482T319%20540Q356%20705%20465%20705Q502%20703%20526%20683T550%20630Q550%20594%20529%20578T487%20561Q443%20561%20443%20603Q443%20622%20454%20636T478%20657L487%20662Q471%20668%20457%20668Q445%20668%20434%20658T419%20630Q412%20601%20403%20552T387%20469T380%20433Q380%20431%20435%20431Q480%20431%20487%20430T498%20424Q499%20420%20496%20407T491%20391Q489%20386%20482%20386T428%20385H372L349%20263Q301%2015%20282%20-47Q255%20-132%20212%20-173Q175%20-205%20139%20-205Q107%20-205%2081%20-186T55%20-132Q55%20-95%2076%20-78T118%20-61Q162%20-61%20162%20-103Q162%20-122%20151%20-136T127%20-157L118%20-162Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMAIN-28%22%20d%3D%22M94%20250Q94%20319%20104%20381T127%20488T164%20576T202%20643T244%20695T277%20729T302%20750H315H319Q333%20750%20333%20741Q333%20738%20316%20720T275%20667T226%20581T184%20443T167%20250T184%2058T225%20-81T274%20-167T316%20-220T333%20-241Q333%20-250%20318%20-250H315H302L274%20-226Q180%20-141%20137%20-14T94%20250Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-78%22%20d%3D%22M52%20289Q59%20331%20106%20386T222%20442Q257%20442%20286%20424T329%20379Q371%20442%20430%20442Q467%20442%20494%20420T522%20361Q522%20332%20508%20314T481%20292T458%20288Q439%20288%20427%20299T415%20328Q415%20374%20465%20391Q454%20404%20425%20404Q412%20404%20406%20402Q368%20386%20350%20336Q290%20115%20290%2078Q290%2050%20306%2038T341%2026Q378%2026%20414%2059T463%20140Q466%20150%20469%20151T485%20153H489Q504%20153%20504%20145Q504%20144%20502%20134Q486%2077%20440%2033T333%20-11Q263%20-11%20227%2052Q186%20-10%20133%20-10H127Q78%20-10%2057%2016T35%2071Q35%20103%2054%20123T99%20143Q142%20143%20142%20101Q142%20 2.1 常数项

对于%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-79%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mo%22%20transform%3D%22translate(775%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMAIN-3D%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%20transform%3D%22translate(1831%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-43%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mo%22%20transform%3D%22translate(2592%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMAIN-2C%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%20transform%3D%22translate(3037%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-43%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mo%22%20transform%3D%22translate(4075%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMAIN-2208%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-texatom%22%20transform%3D%22translate(5020%2C0)%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJAMS-52%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)这样的常数函数：

根据周期函数的定义，常数函数是周期函数，周期为任意实数。

所以，分解里面得有一个常数项。

2.2 通过sin(x),cos(x)进行分解

首先，%2Ccos(x)%3C%2Ftitle%3E%0A%3Cdefs%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-73%22%20d%3D%22M131%20289Q131%20321%20147%20354T203%20415T300%20442Q362%20442%20390%20415T419%20355Q419%20323%20402%20308T364%20292Q351%20292%20340%20300T328%20326Q328%20342%20337%20354T354%20372T367%20378Q368%20378%20368%20379Q368%20382%20361%20388T336%20399T297%20405Q249%20405%20227%20379T204%20326Q204%20301%20223%20291T278%20274T330%20259Q396%20230%20396%20163Q396%20135%20385%20107T352%2051T289%207T195%20-10Q118%20-10%2086%2019T53%2087Q53%20126%2074%20143T118%20160Q133%20160%20146%20151T160%20120Q160%2094%20142%2076T111%2058Q109%2057%20108%2057T107%2055Q108%2052%20115%2047T146%2034T201%2027Q237%2027%20263%2038T301%2066T318%2097T323%20122Q323%20150%20302%20164T254%20181T195%20196T148%20231Q131%20256%20131%20289Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-69%22%20d%3D%22M184%20600Q184%20624%20203%20642T247%20661Q265%20661%20277%20649T290%20619Q290%20596%20270%20577T226%20557Q211%20557%20198%20567T184%20600ZM21%20287Q21%20295%2030%20318T54%20369T98%20420T158%20442Q197%20442%20223%20419T250%20357Q250%20340%20236%20301T196%20196T154%2083Q149%2061%20149%2051Q149%2026%20166%2026Q175%2026%20185%2029T208%2043T235%2078T260%20137Q263%20149%20265%20151T282%20153Q302%20153%20302%20143Q302%20135%20293%20112T268%2061T223%2011T161%20-11Q129%20-11%20102%2010T74%2074Q74%2091%2079%20106T122%20220Q160%20321%20166%20341T173%20380Q173%20404%20156%20404H154Q124%20404%2099%20371T61%20287Q60%20286%2059%20284T58%20281T56%20279T53%20278T49%20278T41%20278H27Q21%20284%2021%20287Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-6E%22%20d%3D%22M21%20287Q22%20293%2024%20303T36%20341T56%20388T89%20425T135%20442Q171%20442%20195%20424T225%20390T231%20369Q231%20367%20232%20367L243%20378Q304%20442%20382%20442Q436%20442%20469%20415T503%20336T465%20179T427%2052Q427%2026%20444%2026Q450%2026%20453%2027Q482%2032%20505%2065T54 函数，进行合理的加减组合，结果可以是周期函数。

其次，它们的微分和积分都很简单。

然后，%3C%2Ftitle%3E%0A%3Cdefs%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-73%22%20d%3D%22M131%20289Q131%20321%20147%20354T203%20415T300%20442Q362%20442%20390%20415T419%20355Q419%20323%20402%20308T364%20292Q351%20292%20340%20300T328%20326Q328%20342%20337%20354T354%20372T367%20378Q368%20378%20368%20379Q368%20382%20361%20388T336%20399T297%20405Q249%20405%20227%20379T204%20326Q204%20301%20223%20291T278%20274T330%20259Q396%20230%20396%20163Q396%20135%20385%20107T352%2051T289%207T195%20-10Q118%20-10%2086%2019T53%2087Q53%20126%2074%20143T118%20160Q133%20160%20146%20151T160%20120Q160%2094%20142%2076T111%2058Q109%2057%20108%2057T107%2055Q108%2052%20115%2047T146%2034T201%2027Q237%2027%20263%2038T301%2066T318%2097T323%20122Q323%20150%20302%20164T254%20181T195%20196T148%20231Q131%20256%20131%20289Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-69%22%20d%3D%22M184%20600Q184%20624%20203%20642T247%20661Q265%20661%20277%20649T290%20619Q290%20596%20270%20577T226%20557Q211%20557%20198%20567T184%20600ZM21%20287Q21%20295%2030%20318T54%20369T98%20420T158%20442Q197%20442%20223%20419T250%20357Q250%20340%20236%20301T196%20196T154%2083Q149%2061%20149%2051Q149%2026%20166%2026Q175%2026%20185%2029T208%2043T235%2078T260%20137Q263%20149%20265%20151T282%20153Q302%20153%20302%20143Q302%20135%20293%20112T268%2061T223%2011T161%20-11Q129%20-11%20102%2010T74%2074Q74%2091%2079%20106T122%20220Q160%20321%20166%20341T173%20380Q173%20404%20156%20404H154Q124%20404%2099%20371T61%20287Q60%20286%2059%20284T58%20281T56%20279T53%20278T49%20278T41%20278H27Q21%20284%2021%20287Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-6E%22%20d%3D%22M21%20287Q22%20293%2024%20303T36%20341T56%20388T89%20425T135%20442Q171%20442%20195%20424T225%20390T231%20369Q231%20367%20232%20367L243%20378Q304%20442%20382%20442Q436%20442%20469%20415T503%20336T465%20179T427%2052Q427%2026%20444%2026Q450%2026%20453%2027Q482%2032%20505%2065T540%20145Q5 从图像上也可以看出，%3C%2Ftitle%3E%0A%3Cdefs%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-73%22%20d%3D%22M131%20289Q131%20321%20147%20354T203%20415T300%20442Q362%20442%20390%20415T419%20355Q419%20323%20402%20308T364%20292Q351%20292%20340%20300T328%20326Q328%20342%20337%20354T354%20372T367%20378Q368%20378%20368%20379Q368%20382%20361%20388T336%20399T297%20405Q249%20405%20227%20379T204%20326Q204%20301%20223%20291T278%20274T330%20259Q396%20230%20396%20163Q396%20135%20385%20107T352%2051T289%207T195%20-10Q118%20-10%2086%2019T53%2087Q53%20126%2074%20143T118%20160Q133%20160%20146%20151T160%20120Q160%2094%20142%2076T111%2058Q109%2057%20108%2057T107%2055Q108%2052%20115%2047T146%2034T201%2027Q237%2027%20263%2038T301%2066T318%2097T323%20122Q323%20150%20302%20164T254%20181T195%20196T148%20231Q131%20256%20131%20289Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-69%22%20d%3D%22M184%20600Q184%20624%20203%20642T247%20661Q265%20661%20277%20649T290%20619Q290%20596%20270%20577T226%20557Q211%20557%20198%20567T184%20600ZM21%20287Q21%20295%2030%20318T54%20369T98%20420T158%20442Q197%20442%20223%20419T250%20357Q250%20340%20236%20301T196%20196T154%2083Q149%2061%20149%2051Q149%2026%20166%2026Q175%2026%20185%2029T208%2043T235%2078T260%20137Q263%20149%20265%20151T282%20153Q302%20153%20302%20143Q302%20135%20293%20112T268%2061T223%2011T161%20-11Q129%20-11%20102%2010T74%2074Q74%2091%2079%20106T122%20220Q160%20321%20166%20341T173%20380Q173%20404%20156%20404H154Q124%20404%2099%20371T61%20287Q60%20286%2059%20284T58%20281T56%20279T53%20278T49%20278T41%20278H27Q21%20284%2021%20287Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-6E%22%20d%3D%22M21%20287Q22%20293%2024%20303T36%20341T56%20388T89%20425T135%20442Q171%20442%20195%20424T225%20390T231%20369Q231%20367%20232%20367L243%20378Q304%20442%20382%20442Q436%20442%20469%20415T503%20336T465%20179T427%2052Q427%2026%20444%2026Q450%2026%20453%2027Q482%2032%20505%2065T540% 而奇函数与奇函数加减只能得到奇函数，即：

其中，%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-msubsup%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-66%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-texatom%22%20transform%3D%22translate(490%2C-150)%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mtext%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20transform%3D%22scale(0.707)%22%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMAIN-6F%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20transform%3D%22scale(0.707)%22%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMAIN-64%22%20x%3D%22500%22%20y%3D%220%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20transform%3D%22scale(0.707)%22%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMAIN-64%22%20x%3D%221057%22%20y%3D%220%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)表示奇函数。

从图像上也可以看出，%3C%2Ftitle%3E%0A%3Cdefs%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-63%22%20d%3D%22M34%20159Q34%20268%20120%20355T306%20442Q362%20442%20394%20418T427%20355Q427%20326%20408%20306T360%20285Q341%20285%20330%20295T319%20325T330%20359T352%20380T366%20386H367Q367%20388%20361%20392T340%20400T306%20404Q276%20404%20249%20390Q228%20381%20206%20359Q162%20315%20142%20235T121%20119Q121%2073%20147%2050Q169%2026%20205%2026H209Q321%2026%20394%20111Q403%20121%20406%20121Q410%20121%20419%20112T429%2098T420%2083T391%2055T346%2025T282%200T202%20-11Q127%20-11%2081%2037T34%20159Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-6F%22%20d%3D%22M201%20-11Q126%20-11%2080%2038T34%20156Q34%20221%2064%20279T146%20380Q222%20441%20301%20441Q333%20441%20341%20440Q354%20437%20367%20433T402%20417T438%20387T464%20338T476%20268Q476%20161%20390%2075T201%20-11ZM121%20120Q121%2070%20147%2048T206%2026Q250%2026%20289%2058T351%20142Q360%20163%20374%20216T388%20308Q388%20352%20370%20375Q346%20405%20306%20405Q243%20405%20195%20347Q158%20303%20140%20230T121%20120Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-73%22%20d%3D%22M131%20289Q131%20321%20147%20354T203%20415T300%20442Q362%20442%20390%20415T419%20355Q419%20323%20402%20308T364%20292Q351%20292%20340%20300T328%20326Q328%20342%20337%20354T354%20372T367%20378Q368%20378%20368%20379Q368%20382%20361%20388T336%20399T297%20405Q249%20405%20227%20379T204%20326Q204%20301%20223%20291T278%20274T330%20259Q396%20230%20396%20163Q396%20135%20385%20107T352%2051T289%207T195%20-10Q118%20-10%2086%2019T53%2087Q53%20126%2074%20143T118%20160Q133%20160%20146%20151T160%20120Q160%2094%20142%2076T111%2058Q109%2057%20108%2057T107%2055Q108%2052%20115%2047T146%2034T201%2027Q237%2027%20263%2038T301%2066T318%2097T323%20122Q323%20150%20302%20164T254%20181T195%20196T148%20231Q131%20256%20131%20289Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMAIN-28%22%20d%3 同样的，偶函数与偶函数加减只能得到偶函数，即：

其中，%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-msubsup%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-66%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-texatom%22%20transform%3D%22translate(490%2C-150)%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mtext%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20transform%3D%22scale(0.707)%22%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMAIN-65%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20transform%3D%22scale(0.707)%22%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMAIN-76%22%20x%3D%22444%22%20y%3D%220%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20transform%3D%22scale(0.707)%22%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMAIN-65%22%20x%3D%22972%22%20y%3D%220%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20transform%3D%22scale(0.707)%22%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMAIN-6E%22%20x%3D%221417%22%20y%3D%220%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)表示偶函数。

但是任意函数可以分解和奇偶函数之和：

所以同时需要%2Ccos(x)%3C%2Ftitle%3E%0A%3Cdefs%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-73%22%20d%3D%22M131%20289Q131%20321%20147%20354T203%20415T300%20442Q362%20442%20390%20415T419%20355Q419%20323%20402%20308T364%20292Q351%20292%20340%20300T328%20326Q328%20342%20337%20354T354%20372T367%20378Q368%20378%20368%20379Q368%20382%20361%20388T336%20399T297%20405Q249%20405%20227%20379T204%20326Q204%20301%20223%20291T278%20274T330%20259Q396%20230%20396%20163Q396%20135%20385%20107T352%2051T289%207T195%20-10Q118%20-10%2086%2019T53%2087Q53%20126%2074%20143T118%20160Q133%20160%20146%20151T160%20120Q160%2094%20142%2076T111%2058Q109%2057%20108%2057T107%2055Q108%2052%20115%2047T146%2034T201%2027Q237%2027%20263%2038T301%2066T318%2097T323%20122Q323%20150%20302%20164T254%20181T195%20196T148%20231Q131%20256%20131%20289Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-69%22%20d%3D%22M184%20600Q184%20624%20203%20642T247%20661Q265%20661%20277%20649T290%20619Q290%20596%20270%20577T226%20557Q211%20557%20198%20567T184%20600ZM21%20287Q21%20295%2030%20318T54%20369T98%20420T158%20442Q197%20442%20223%20419T250%20357Q250%20340%20236%20301T196%20196T154%2083Q149%2061%20149%2051Q149%2026%20166%2026Q175%2026%20185%2029T208%2043T235%2078T260%20137Q263%20149%20265%20151T282%20153Q302%20153%20302%20143Q302%20135%20293%20112T268%2061T223%2011T161%20-11Q129%20-11%20102%2010T74%2074Q74%2091%2079%20106T122%20220Q160%20321%20166%20341T173%20380Q173%20404%20156%20404H154Q124%20404%2099%20371T61%20287Q60%20286%2059%20284T58%20281T56%20279T53%20278T49%20278T41%20278H27Q21%20284%2021%20287Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-6E%22%20d%3D%22M21%20287Q22%20293%2024%20303T36%20341T56%20388T89%20425T135%20442Q171%20442%20195%20424T225%20390T231%20369Q231%20367%20232%20367L243%20378Q304%20442%20382%20442Q436%20442%20469%20415T503%20336T465%20179T427%2052Q427%2026%20444%2026Q450%2026%20453%2027Q482%2032%20505%2065 。

2.3 保证组合出来周期为T

之前说了，%3C%2Ftitle%3E%0A%3Cdefs%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-66%22%20d%3D%22M118%20-162Q120%20-162%20124%20-164T135%20-167T147%20-168Q160%20-168%20171%20-155T187%20-126Q197%20-99%20221%2027T267%20267T289%20382V385H242Q195%20385%20192%20387Q188%20390%20188%20397L195%20425Q197%20430%20203%20430T250%20431Q298%20431%20298%20432Q298%20434%20307%20482T319%20540Q356%20705%20465%20705Q502%20703%20526%20683T550%20630Q550%20594%20529%20578T487%20561Q443%20561%20443%20603Q443%20622%20454%20636T478%20657L487%20662Q471%20668%20457%20668Q445%20668%20434%20658T419%20630Q412%20601%20403%20552T387%20469T380%20433Q380%20431%20435%20431Q480%20431%20487%20430T498%20424Q499%20420%20496%20407T491%20391Q489%20386%20482%20386T428%20385H372L349%20263Q301%2015%20282%20-47Q255%20-132%20212%20-173Q175%20-205%20139%20-205Q107%20-205%2081%20-186T55%20-132Q55%20-95%2076%20-78T118%20-61Q162%20-61%20162%20-103Q162%20-122%20151%20-136T127%20-157L118%20-162Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMAIN-28%22%20d%3D%22M94%20250Q94%20319%20104%20381T127%20488T164%20576T202%20643T244%20695T277%20729T302%20750H315H319Q333%20750%20333%20741Q333%20738%20316%20720T275%20667T226%20581T184%20443T167%20250T184%2058T225%20-81T274%20-167T316%20-220T333%20-241Q333%20-250%20318%20-250H315H302L274%20-226Q180%20-141%20137%20-14T94%20250Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-78%22%20d%3D%22M52%20289Q59%20331%20106%20386T222%20442Q257%20442%20286%20424T329%20379Q371%20442%20430%20442Q467%20442%20494%20420T522%20361Q522%20332%20508%20314T481%20292T458%20288Q439%20288%20427%20299T415%20328Q415%20374%20465%20391Q454%20404%20425%20404Q412%20404%20406%20402Q368%20386%20350%20336Q290%20115%20290%2078Q290%2050%20306%2038T341%2026Q378%2026%20414%2059T463%20140Q466%20150%20469%20151T485%20153H489Q504%20153%20504%20145Q504%20144%20502%20134Q486%2077%20440%2033T333%20-11Q263%20-11%20227%2052Q186%20-10%20133%20-10H127Q78%20-10%2057%2016T35%2071Q35%20103%2054%20123T99%20143Q142%20143%20142%20101Q142%2081%20130%2066T107%2046T94%2041L91%2040Q91%2039%2097%2036T113%2029T132%2026Q168%2026%20194%2071Q203%2087%20217%20139T245%20247T261%20313Q266%20340%20266%20352Q266%20380%20251%20392T217%20404Q177%20404%20142%20372T93%20290Q91%20281%2088%20280T72%20278H58Q52%20284%2052%20289Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMAIN-29%22%20d%3D%22M60%20749L64%20750Q69%20750%2074%20750H86L114%20726Q208%20641%20251%20514T294%20250Q294%20182%20284%20119T261%2012T224%20-76T186%20-143T145%20-194T113%20-227T90%20-246Q87%20-249%2086%20-250H74Q66%20-250%2063%20-250T58%20-247T55%20-238Q56%20-237%2066%20-225Q221%20-64%20221%20250T66%20725Q56%20737%2055%20738Q55%20746%2060%20749Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3C%2Fdefs%3E%0A%3Cg%20stroke%3D%22currentColor%22%20fill%3D%22currentColor%22%20stroke-width%3D%220%22%20transform%3D%22matrix(1%200%200%20-1%200%200)%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-66%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mo%22%20transform%3D%22translate(550%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMAIN-28%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%20transform%3D%22translate(940%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-78%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mo%22%20transform%3D%22translate(1512%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMAIN-29%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)是周期为%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-54%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)的函数，我们怎么保证组合出来的函数周期依然为%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-54%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)呢？

比如下面这个函数的周期为%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mn%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMAIN-32%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%20transform%3D%22translate(500%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-3C0%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)：

很显然，%3C%2Ftitle%3E%0A%3Cdefs%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-73%22%20d%3D%22M131%20289Q131%20321%20147%20354T203%20415T300%20442Q362%20442%20390%20415T419%20355Q419%20323%20402%20308T364%20292Q351%20292%20340%20300T328%20326Q328%20342%20337%20354T354%20372T367%20378Q368%20378%20368%20379Q368%20382%20361%20388T336%20399T297%20405Q249%20405%20227%20379T204%20326Q204%20301%20223%20291T278%20274T330%20259Q396%20230%20396%20163Q396%20135%20385%20107T352%2051T289%207T195%20-10Q118%20-10%2086%2019T53%2087Q53%20126%2074%20143T118%20160Q133%20160%20146%20151T160%20120Q160%2094%20142%2076T111%2058Q109%2057%20108%2057T107%2055Q108%2052%20115%2047T146%2034T201%2027Q237%2027%20263%2038T301%2066T318%2097T323%20122Q323%20150%20302%20164T254%20181T195%20196T148%20231Q131%20256%20131%20289Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-69%22%20d%3D%22M184%20600Q184%20624%20203%20642T247%20661Q265%20661%20277%20649T290%20619Q290%20596%20270%20577T226%20557Q211%20557%20198%20567T184%20600ZM21%20287Q21%20295%2030%20318T54%20369T98%20420T158%20442Q197%20442%20223%20419T250%20357Q250%20340%20236%20301T196%20196T154%2083Q149%2061%20149%2051Q149%2026%20166%2026Q175%2026%20185%2029T208%2043T235%2078T260%20137Q263%20149%20265%20151T282%20153Q302%20153%20302%20143Q302%20135%20293%20112T268%2061T223%2011T161%20-11Q129%20-11%20102%2010T74%2074Q74%2091%2079%20106T122%20220Q160%20321%20166%20341T173%20380Q173%20404%20156%20404H154Q124%20404%2099%20371T61%20287Q60%20286%2059%20284T58%20281T56%20279T53%20278T49%20278T41%20278H27Q21%20284%2021%20287Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-6E%22%20d%3D%22M21%20287Q22%20293%2024%20303T36%20341T56%20388T89%20425T135%20442Q171%20442%20195%20424T225%20390T231%20369Q231%20367%20232%20367L243%20378Q304%20442%20382%20442Q436%20442%20469%20415T503%20336T465%20179T427%2052Q427%2026%20444%2026Q450%2026%20453%2027Q482%2032%20505%2065T540%20145Q %20-10H127Q78%20-10%2057%2016T35%2071Q35%20103%2054%20123T99%20143Q142%20143%20142%20101Q142%2081%20130%2066T107%2046T94%2041L91%2040Q91%2039%2097%2036T113%2029T132%2026Q168%2026%20194%2071Q203%2087%20217%20139T245%20247T261%20313Q266%20340%20266%20352Q266%20380%20251%20392T217%20404Q177%20404%20142%20372T93%20290Q91%20281%2088%20280T72%20278H58Q52%20284%2052%20289Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMAIN-29%22%20d%3D%22M60%20749L64%20750Q69%20750%2074%20750H86L114%20726Q208%20641%20251%20514T294%20250Q294%20182%20284%20119T261%2012T224%20-76T186%20-143T145%20-194T113%20-227T90%20-246Q87%20-249%2086%20-250H74Q66%20-250%2063%20-250T58%20-247T55%20-238Q56%20-237%2066%20-225Q221%20-64%20221%20250T66%20725Q56%20737%2055%20738Q55%20746%2060%20749Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3C%2Fdefs%3E%0A%3Cg%20stroke%3D%22currentColor%22%20fill%3D%22currentColor%22%20stroke-width%3D%220%22%20transform%3D%22matrix(1%200%200%20-1%200%200)%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-66%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mo%22%20transform%3D%22translate(550%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMAIN-28%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%20transform%3D%22translate(940%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-78%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mo%22%20transform%3D%22translate(1512%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMAIN-29%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)的周期为%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-54%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)，那么：

这些函数的周期都为%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-54%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)。

将这些函数进行加减，就保证了得到的函数的周期也为%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-54%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)。

2.4 调整振幅

现在我们有一堆周期为%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mn%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMAIN-32%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%20transform%3D%22translate(500%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-3C0%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)的函数了，比如说%2Csin(2x)%2Csin(3x)%2Csin(4x)%2Csin(5x)%3C%2Ftitle%3E%0A%3Cdefs%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-73%22%20d%3D%22M131%20289Q131%20321%20147%20354T203%20415T300%20442Q362%20442%20390%20415T419%20355Q419%20323%20402%20308T364%20292Q351%20292%20340%20300T328%20326Q328%20342%20337%20354T354%20372T367%20378Q368%20378%20368%20379Q368%20382%20361%20388T336%20399T297%20405Q249%20405%20227%20379T204%20326Q204%20301%20223%20291T278%20274T330%20259Q396%20230%20396%20163Q396%20135%20385%20107T352%2051T289%207T195%20-10Q118%20-10%2086%2019T53%2087Q53%20126%2074%20143T118%20160Q133%20160%20146%20151T160%20120Q160%2094%20142%2076T111%2058Q109%2057%20108%2057T107%2055Q108%2052%20115%2047T146%2034T201%2027Q237%2027%20263%2038T301%2066T318%2097T323%20122Q323%20150%20302%20164T254%20181T195%20196T148%20231Q131%20256%20131%20289Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-69%22%20d%3D%22M184%20600Q184%20624%20203%20642T247%20661Q265%20661%20277%20649T290%20619Q290%20596%20270%20577T226%20557Q211%20557%20198%20567T184%20600ZM21%20287Q21%20295%2030%20318T54%20369T98%20420T158%20442Q197%20442%20223%20419T250%20357Q250%20340%20236%20301T196%20196T154%2083Q149%2061%20149%2051Q149%2026%20166%2026Q175%2026%20185%2029T208%2043T235%2078T260%20137Q263%20149%20265%20151T282%20153Q302%20153%20302%20143Q302%20135%20293%20112T268%2061T223%2011T161%20-11Q129%20-11%20102%2010T74%2074Q74%2091%2079%20106T122%20220Q160%20321%20166%20341T173%20380Q173%20404%20156%20404H154Q124%20404%2099%20371T61%20287Q60%20286%2059%20284T58 把它的振幅增加一倍：

调整振幅，加加减减，我们可以慢慢接近目标函数：

2.5 小结

综上，构造出来的三角函数之和大概类似下面的样子：

这样就符合之前的分析：

  • 有常数项
  • 奇函数和偶函数可以组合出任意函数
  • 周期为%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-54%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)
  • 调整振幅，逼近原函数

之前的分析还比较简单，后面开始有点难度了。即怎么确定这三个系数：

3 sin(x)的另外一种表示方法

直接不好确定，要迂回一下，先稍微介绍一下什么是：%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-msubsup%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-65%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-texatom%22%20transform%3D%22translate(466%2C412)%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20transform%3D%22scale(0.707)%22%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-69%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%20transform%3D%22translate(244%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20transform%3D%22scale(0.707)%22%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-3C9%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%20transform%3D%22translate(684%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20transform%3D%22scale(0.707)%22%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-74%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)？

3.1 eiwt

看到类似于%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-msubsup%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-65%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-texatom%22%20transform%3D%22translate(466%2C412)%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20transform%3D%22scale(0.707)%22%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-69%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%20transform%3D%22translate(244%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20transform%3D%22scale(0.707)%22%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-3B8%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)这种就应该想到复平面上的一个夹角为%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-3B8%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)的向量：

那么当%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-3B8%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)不再是常数，而是代表时间的变量%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-74%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)的时候：

%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-msubsup%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-65%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-texatom%22%20transform%3D%22translate(466%2C412)%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20transform%3D%22scale(0.707)%22%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-69%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%20transform%3D%22translate(244%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20transform%3D%22scale(0.707)%22%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-3B8%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mo%22%20transform%3D%22translate(1420%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMAIN-2192%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-msubsup%22%20transform%3D%22translate(2698%2C0)%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-65%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-texatom%22%20transform%3D%22translate(466%2C412)%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20transform%3D%22scale(0.707)%22%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-69%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-texatom%22%20transform%3D%22translate(244%2C0)%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20fill%3D%22red%22%20stroke%3D%22red%22%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mstyle%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20fill%3D%22red%22%20stroke%3D%22red%22%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20fill%3D%22red%22%20stroke%3D%22red%22%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20transform%3D%22scale(0.707)%22%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-74%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)

随着时间%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-74%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)的流逝，从0开始增长，这个向量就会旋转起来，%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mn%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMAIN-32%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%20transform%3D%22translate(500%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-3C0%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)秒会旋转一圈，也就是%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-54%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mo%22%20transform%3D%22translate(982%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMAIN-3D%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mn%22%20transform%3D%22translate(2038%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMAIN-32%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%20transform%3D%22translate(2539%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-3C0%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)：

3.2 通过eiwt表示sin(t)

根据欧拉公式，有：

%2Bisin(t)%3C%2Ftitle%3E%0A%3Cdefs%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-65%22%20d%3D%22M39%20168Q39%20225%2058%20272T107%20350T174%20402T244%20433T307%20442H310Q355%20442%20388%20420T421%20355Q421%20265%20310%20237Q261%20224%20176%20223Q139%20223%20138%20221Q138%20219%20132%20186T125%20128Q125%2081%20146%2054T209%2026T302%2045T394%20111Q403%20121%20406%20121Q410%20121%20419%20112T429%2098T420%2082T390%2055T344%2024T281%20-1T205%20-11Q126%20-11%2083%2042T39%20168ZM373%20353Q367%20405%20305%20405Q272%20405%20244%20391T199%20357T170%20316T154%20280T149%20261Q149%20260%20169%20260Q282%20260%20327%20284T373%20353Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-69%22%20d%3D%22M184%20600Q184%20624%20203%20642T247%20661Q265%20661%20277%20649T290%20619Q290%20596%20270%20577T226%20557Q211%20557%20198%20567T184%20600ZM21%20287Q21%20295%2030%20318T54%20369T98%20420T158%20442Q197%20442%20223%20419T250%20357Q250%20340%20236%20301T196%20196T154%2083Q149%2061%20149%2051Q149%2026%20166%2026Q175%2026%20185%2029T208%2043T235%2078T260%20137Q263%20149%20265%20151T282%20153Q302%20153%20302%20143Q302%20135%20293%20112T268%2061T223%2011T161%20-11Q129%20-11%20102%2010T74%2074Q74%2091%2079%20106T122%20220Q160%20321%20166%20341T173%20380Q173%20404%20156%20404H154Q124%20404%2099%20371T61%20287Q60%20286%2059%20284T58%20281T56%20279T53%20278T49%20278T41%20278H27Q21%20284%2021%20287Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-74%22%20d%3D%22M26%20385Q19%20392%2019%20395Q19%20399%2022%20411T27%20425Q29%20430%2036%20430T87%20431H140L159%20511Q162%20522%20166%20540T173%20566T179%20586T187%20603T197%20615T211%20624T229%20626Q247%20625%20254%20615T261%20596Q261%20589%20252%20549T232%20470L222%20433Q222%20431%20272%20431H323Q330%20424%20330%20420Q330%20398%20317%20385H210L174%20240Q135%2080%20135%2068Q135%2026%20162%2026Q197%2026%20230%2060T283%20144Q285%20150%20288%20151T303%20153H307Q322%20153 所以，在时间%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-74%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)轴上，把%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-msubsup%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-65%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-texatom%22%20transform%3D%22translate(466%2C412)%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20transform%3D%22scale(0.707)%22%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-69%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%20transform%3D%22translate(244%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20transform%3D%22scale(0.707)%22%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-74%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)向量的虚部（也就是纵坐标）记录下来，得到的就是%3C%2Ftitle%3E%0A%3Cdefs%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-73%22%20d%3D%22M131%20289Q131%20321%20147%20354T203%20415T300%20442Q362%20442%20390%20415T419%20355Q419%20323%20402%20308T364%20292Q351%20292%20340%20300T328%20326Q328%20342%20337%20354T354%20372T367%20378Q368%20378%20368%20379Q368%20382%20361%20388T336%20399T297%20405Q249%20405%20227%20379T204%20326Q204%20301%20223%20291T278%20274T330%20259Q396%20230%20396%20163Q396%20135%20385%20107T352%2051T289%207T195%20-10Q118%20-10%2086%2019T53%2087Q53%20126%2074%20143T118%20160Q133%20160%20146%20151T160%20120Q160%2094%20142%2076T111%2058Q109%2057%20108%2057T107%2055Q108%2052%20115%2047T146%2034T201%2027Q237%2027%20263%2038T301%2066T318%2097T323%20122Q323%20150%20302%20164T254%20181T195%20196T148%20231Q131%20256%20131%20289Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-69%22%20d%3D%22M184%20600Q184%20624%20203%20642T247%2 这两种角度，一个可以观察到旋转的频率，所以称为频域；一个可以看到流逝的时间，所以称为时域：

4 通过频域来求系数

4.1 函数是线性组合

假设有这么个函数：

是一个%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-54%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mo%22%20transform%3D%22translate(982%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMAIN-3D%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mn%22%20transform%3D%22translate(2038%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMAIN-32%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%20transform%3D%22translate(2539%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-3C0%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)的函数：

如果转到频域去，那么它们是下面这个复数函数的虚部：

先看看%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-msubsup%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-65%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-texatom%22%20transform%3D%22translate(466%2C412)%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20transform%3D%22scale(0.707)%22%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-69%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%20transform%3D%22translate(244%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20transform%3D%22scale(0.707)%22%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-3B8%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mo%22%20transform%3D%22translate(1365%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMAIN-2B%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-msubsup%22%20transform%3D%22translate(2365%2C0)%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-65%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-texatom%22%20transform%3D%22translate(466%2C412)%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20transform%3D%22scale(0.707)%22%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-69%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mn%22%20transform%3D%22translate(244%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20transform%3D%22scale(0.707)%22%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMAIN-32%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%20transform%3D%22translate(598%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20transform%3D%22scale(0.707)%22%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-3B8%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)，其中%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-3B8%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3 现在让它们动起来，把%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-3B8%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)变成流逝的时间%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-74%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)，并且把虚部记录下来：

我们令：

这里用大写的%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-47%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)来表示复数函数。

刚才看到了，%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-msubsup%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-65%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-texatom%22%20transform%3D%22translate(466%2C412)%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20transform%3D%22scale(0.707)%22%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-69%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%20transform%3D%22translate(244%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20transform%3D%22scale(0.707)%22%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-74%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)和%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-msubsup%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-65%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-texatom%22%20transform%3D%22translate(466%2C412)%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20transform%3D%22scale(0.707)%22%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-69%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mn%22%20transform%3D%22translate(244%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20transform%3D%22scale(0.707)%22%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMAIN-32%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mi%22%20transform%3D%22translate(598%2C0)%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20transform%3D%22scale(0.707)%22%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMATHI-74%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)都是向量，所以上式可以写作：

%7D%3D%5Cvec%7Be%5E%7Bit%7D%7D%2B%5Cvec%7Be%5E%7Bi2t%7D%7D%3C%2Ftitle%3E%0A%3Cdefs%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-47%22%20d%3D%22M50%20252Q50%20367%20117%20473T286%20641T490%20704Q580%20704%20633%20653Q642%20643%20648%20636T656%20626L657%20623Q660%20623%20684%20649Q691%20655%20699%20663T715%20679T725%20690L740%20705H746Q760%20705%20760%20698Q760%20694%20728%20561Q692%20422%20692%20421Q690%20416%20687%20415T669%20413H653Q647%20419%20647%20422Q647%20423%20648%20429T650%20449T651%20481Q651%20552%20619%20605T510%20659Q492%20659%20471%20656T418%20643T357%20615T294%20567T236%20496T189%20394T158%20260Q156%20242%20156%20221Q156%20173%20170%20136T206%2079T256%2045T308%2028T353%2024Q407%2024%20452%2047T514%20106Q517%20114%20529%20161T541%20214Q541%20222%20528%20224T468%20227H431Q425%20233%20425%20235T427%20254Q431%20267%20437%20273H454Q494%20271%20594%20271Q634%20271%20659%20271T695%20272T707%20272Q721%20272%20721%20263Q721%20261%20719%20249Q714%20230%20709%20228Q706%20227%20694%20227Q674%20227%20653%20224Q646%20221%20643%20215T629%20164Q620%20131%20614%20108Q589%206%20586%203Q584%201%20581%201Q571%201%20553%2021T530%2052Q530%2053%20528%2052T522%2047Q448%20-22%20322%20-22Q201%20-22%20126%2055T50%20252Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMAIN-28%22%20d%3D%22M94%20250Q94%20319%20104%20381T127%20488T164%20576T202%20643T244%20695T277%20729T302%20750H315H319Q333%20750%20333%20741Q333%20738%20316%20720T275%20667T226%20581T184%20443T167%20250T184%2058T225%20-81T274%20-167T316%20-220T333%20-241Q333%20-250%20318%20-250H315H302L274%20-226Q180%20-141%20137%20-14T94%20250Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-74%22%20d%3D%22M26%20385Q19%20392%2019%20395Q19%20399%2022%20411T27%20425Q29%20430%2036%20430T87%20431H140L159%20511Q162%20522%20166%20540T173%20566T179%20586T187%20603T197%20615T211%20624T229%20626Q247%20625%20254%20615T261%20596Q261%20589%20252%20549T232%2 这里就是理解的重点了，从线性代数的角度：

4.2 如何求正交基的坐标

有了这个结论之后，我们如何求坐标？

我们来看个例子，假设：

通过点积：

可知这两个向量正交，是正交基。图示如下：

4.3 如何求sin(nt)基下的坐标

在这里抛出一个结论（可以参考无限维的希尔伯特空间,自行google），函数向量的点积是这么定义的：

4.4 更一般的

对于我们之前的假设，其中%3C%2Ftitle%3E%0A%3Cdefs%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-66%22%20d%3D%22M118%20-162Q120%20-162%20124%20-164T135%20-167T147%20-168Q160%20-168%20171%20-155T187%20-126Q197%20-99%20221%2027T267%20267T289%20382V385H242Q195%20385%20192%20387Q188%20390%20188%20397L195%20425Q197%20430%20203%20430T250%20431Q298%20431%20298%20432Q298%20434%20307%20482T319%20540Q356%20705%20465%20705Q502%20703%20526%20683T550%20630Q550%20594%20529%20578T487%20561Q443%20561%20443%20603Q443%20622%20454%20636T478%20657L487%20662Q471%20668%20457%20668Q445%20668%20434%20658T419%20630Q412%20601%20403%20552T387%20469T380%20433Q380%20431%20435%20431Q480%20431%20487%20430T498%20424Q499%20420%20496%20407T491%20391Q489%20386%20482%20386T428%20385H372L349%20263Q301%2015%20282%20-47Q255%20-132%20212%20-173Q175%20-205%20139%20-205Q107%20-205%2081%20-186T55%20-132Q55%20-95%2076%20-78T118%20-61Q162%20-61%20162%20-103Q162%20-122%20151%20-136T127%20-157L118%20-162Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMAIN-28%22%20d%3D%22M94%20250Q94%20319%20104%20381T127%20488T164%20576T202%20643T244%20695T277%20729T302%20750H315H319Q333%20750%20333%20741Q333%20738%20316%20720T275%20667T226%20581T184%20443T167%20250T184%2058T225%20-81T274%20-167T316%20-220T333%20-241Q333%20-250%20318%20-250H315H302L274%20-226Q180%20-141%20137%20-14T94%20250Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-78%22%20d%3D%22M52%20289Q59%20331%20106%20386T222%20442Q257%20442%20286%20424T329%20379Q371%20442%20430%20442Q467%20442%20494%20420T522%20361Q522%20332%20508%20314T481%20292T458%20288Q439%20288%20427%20299T415%20328Q415%20374%20465%20391Q454%20404%20425%20404Q412%20404%20406%20402Q368%20386%20350%20336Q290%20115%20290%2078Q290%2050%20306%2038T341%2026Q378%2026%20414%2059T463%20140Q466%20150%20469%20151T485%20153H489Q504%20153%20504%20145Q504%20144%20502%20134Q486%2077%20440%2033T333%20-11Q263%20-11%20227%2052Q186%20-10% 可以改写为这样：

也就是说向量%3C%2Ftitle%3E%0A%3Cdefs%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-66%22%20d%3D%22M118%20-162Q120%20-162%20124%20-164T135%20-167T147%20-168Q160%20-168%20171%20-155T187%20-126Q197%20-99%20221%2027T267%20267T289%20382V385H242Q195%20385%20192%20387Q188%20390%20188%20397L195%20425Q197%20430%20203%20430T250%20431Q298%20431%20298%20432Q298%20434%20307%20482T319%20540Q356%20705%20465%20705Q502%20703%20526%20683T550%20630Q550%20594%20529%20578T487%20561Q443%20561%20443%20603Q443%20622%20454%20636T478%20657L487%20662Q471%20668%20457%20668Q445%20668%20434%20658T419%20630Q412%20601%20403%20552T387%20469T380%20433Q380%20431%20435%20431Q480%20431%20487%20430T498%20424Q499%20420%20496%20407T491%20391Q489%20386%20482%20386T428%20385H372L349%20263Q301%2015%20282%20-47Q255%20-132%20212%20-173Q175%20-205%20139%20-205Q107%20-205%2081%20-186T55%20-132Q55%20-95%2076%20-78T118%20-61Q162%20-61%20162%20-103Q162%20-122%20151%20-136T127%20-157L118%20-162Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMAIN-28%22%20d%3D%22M94%20250Q94%20319%20104%20381T127%20488T164%20576T202%20643T244%20695T277%20729T302%20750H315H319Q333%20750%20333%20741Q333%20738%20316%20720T275%20667T226%20581T184%20443T167%20250T184%2058T225%20-81T274%20-167T316%20-220T333%20-241Q333%20-250%20318%20-250H315H302L274%20-226Q180%20-141%20137%20-14T94%20250Z%22%3E%3C%2Fpath%3E%0A%3Cpath%20stroke-width%3D%221%22%20id%3D%22E1-MJMATHI-78%22%20d%3D%22M52%20289Q59%20331%20106%20386T222%20442Q257%20442%20286%20424T329%20379Q371%20442%20430%20442Q467%20442%20494%20420T522%20361Q522%20332%20508%20314T481%20292T458%20288Q439%20288%20427%20299T415%20328Q415%20374%20465%20391Q454%20404%20425%20404Q412%20404%20406%20402Q368%20386%20350%20336Q290%20115%20290%2078Q290%2050%20306%2038T341%2026Q378%2026%20414%2059T463%20140Q466%20150%20469%20151T485%20153H489Q504%20153%20504%20145Q504%20144%20502%20134Q486%2077%20440%2033T333%20-11Q263%20-11%20227%2052Q186%20-10%20133% 是的，%22%20aria-hidden%3D%22true%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mrow%22%3E%0A%3Cg%20class%3D%22mjx-svg-mn%22%3E%0A%20%3Cuse%20xlink%3Ahref%3D%22%23E1-MJMAIN-31%22%3E%3C%2Fuse%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E)也是基。

那么可以得到：
